# Time

* [Edit source](/wiki/Time?action=edit)

| [This article covers the Canon version of this subject.](/wiki/Time "This article covers the Canon version of this subject.") |  | [Click here for Wookieepedia's article on the Legends version of this subject.](/wiki/Time/Legends "Click here for Wookieepedia's article on the Legends version of this subject.") |  |

[![OnACanonArticle](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](/wiki/Canon "Canon")[![GoToLegends](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](/wiki/Time/Legends "Time/Legends")

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| |  |  | | --- | --- | | [Z-95 Headhunter](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4c/Z-95_Headhunter.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20080821014929) | Content approaching. *[Queen's Shadow](/wiki/Queen%27s_Shadow "Queen's Shadow")*–class.  Parts of this article are no longer up to date.  Please update the article to include missing information, and remove this template when finished. | |  |

:   "Time*. That's what's* left *when you strip away everything else.* […] *From a certain perspective, time's the only thing a thief ever* really *steals. And it's the only* gift *an irredeemable disaster can give to anyone.*"
:   ―[Chelli Lona Aphra](/wiki/Chelli_Lona_Aphra "Chelli Lona Aphra")[[1]](#cite_note-Aphra_2016_40-1)

 [![ could be used to measure time.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/11/Hourglass.png/revision/latest?cb=20250123224832) [![ could be used to measure time.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/11/Hourglass.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20250123224832)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/11/Hourglass.png/revision/latest?cb=20250123224832) 

[Hourglasses](/wiki/Hourglass "Hourglass") could be used to measure time.

 

**Time** was a measurable part of the structure of the [universe](/wiki/Universe "Universe"), in which [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") existed, where events occurred in a sequence. Time was measured with different concepts, such as [millennia](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium"), [centuries](/wiki/Standard_century "Standard century"), and [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year"). Time could be broken down even further into [months](/wiki/Standard_month "Standard month"), [weeks](/wiki/Standard_week "Standard week"), [days](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day"), [hours](/wiki/Standard_hour "Standard hour"), [minutes](/wiki/Standard_minute "Standard minute"), and [seconds](/wiki/Second "Second"), though these divisions were used almost exclusively to refer to the duration of events, rather than the date or time on which they took place. [Chronometers](/wiki/Chronometer "Chronometer") were used to track and indicate time through such units of measurement.[[2]](#cite_note-Weapons_Factory-2)

[Time travel](/wiki/Time_travel "Time travel") was a mostly hypothetical method of travel through time.[[3]](#cite_note-Rebels-3) When traveling through hyperspace, the passage of time sped up, and [Stasis fields](/wiki/Stasis_field "Stasis field") were used to slow down time to match the rest of [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy").[[4]](#cite_note-Complete_Vehicles,_New_Edition-4) Time flowed differently in [the Veil](/wiki/The_Veil_(Planet_X) "The Veil (Planet X)") than in normal space.[[5]](#cite_note-Path_Ven-5)

## Time keeping[]

### Overview[]

:   "*Time, time, there's no* time *for time.*"
:   ―[Inspector](/wiki/Inspector "Inspector") [Tanivos Exantor Divo](/wiki/Tanivos_Exantor_Divo "Tanivos Exantor Divo")[[6]](#cite_note-Senate_Murders-6)

The last great conflict between the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") and the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") resulted in a definitive Republic victory. Resetting its [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"), history reset its chrono on this date from which the modern Galactic Republic was born. The time before this rebirth was forgotten as a dark age, lumped into a collective whole known as the "[Old Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic")." As a result of this change, official calendars reset their zero year onto this date.[[7]](#cite_note-Propaganda-7) The galaxy used this standardized dating system based off of the galactic capital Coruscant:[[8]](#cite_note-Future_of_the_Force_Recon-8) the [galactic standard calendar](/wiki/Galactic_standard_calendar "Galactic standard calendar"). On Coruscant, a year was made up of 365 days of 24 hours each,[[9]](#cite_note-AEYNK-9) with no leap years.[[10]](#cite_note-SWCE_2016_DK_Books_Liveblog-10)

During its [reign](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"), the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") reset the dating system and utilized its own [calendar](/wiki/Imperial_calendar "Imperial calendar").[[11]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-11) Sometime after the [Battle of Yavin](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin"), [Ithorian](/wiki/Ithorian "Ithorian") [artist](/wiki/Artist "Artist") [Gammit Chond](/wiki/Gammit_Chond "Gammit Chond") used a [calendar system](/wiki/Galactic_standard_calendar "Galactic standard calendar") that used the battle as the zero year from which to date galactic history. Dates before the Battle of Yavin were marked "BBY" and dates after the Battle of Yavin were marked "ABY."[[12]](#cite_note-GA-12) [Galactic Standard Time](/wiki/Galactic_Standard_Time "Galactic Standard Time") was a system of timekeeping used by the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order").[[13]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_Episode_VII_The_Force_Awakens-13) [Lothal](/wiki/Lothal "Lothal") also maintained its own [calendar](/wiki/Lothal_Calendar "Lothal Calendar").[[9]](#cite_note-AEYNK-9)

### Units of time[]

The most commonly used measurements of time in the Galaxy were the **day** and the **year**, both based on the orbital characteristics of Coruscant.[[8]](#cite_note-Future_of_the_Force_Recon-8) The day was based on its rotational period, and the year was based on its orbital period which, due to a convenient coincidence, was *exactly* 365 times its rotational period. The day was subdivided into 24 **hour**s.[[14]](#cite_note-AB_Update-14) A minute was 60 **second**s.[[15]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_(2020)_18-15)

### Ancient time keeping methods[]

Long before the modern Galactic Republic, the [Domancion Accord](/wiki/Domancion_Accord "Domancion Accord") was used as the zero year for an ancient dating system.[[16]](#cite_note-Doctor_Aphra_6-16)

The [C.R.C.](/wiki/Coruscant_reckoning_calendar "Coruscant reckoning calendar") was another dating system that set its epoch 7977 years before the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") issued an arrest warrant for [Princess](/wiki/Princess "Princess") [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo") after discovering she worked with the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic").[[17]](#cite_note-Scum_and_Villainy_Case_Files-17)
